class=\"widenode\">\n\t    \n    \n\n\n\n\n\n<article role=\"article\" about=\"/node/19\" class=\"section full clearfix nodenid19 node\">\n\n        \n        <div class=\"node-container\">\n            <div class=\"container\">\n                                                                                                    <div class=\"row\">\n                                        <div class=\"node-content col-sm-8\">\n                        \n                                                    <div class=\"node-title\">\n                                                                    <h1 class=\"js-quickedit-page-title page-header\">Graduate All Students Ready for College and Career Success</h1>\n                                                            </div>\n                                                \n                        <div class=\"content\">\n                            \n            <div class=\"field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field--item\"><p>Are you able to meet the needs of all your students—from those struggling in their coursework to those capable of accelerating their learning?&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>\n\n<p>If you're like most educators, the answer is likely no. It's a challenge to address the diverse learning needs of all students.</p>\n\n<p>This is where Apex Learning comes in. Digital curriculum to personalize learning, actionable&nbsp;data to inform instruction, and success management combine to ensure your students are learning and you get the results you're expecting.</p>\n\n<p><a class=\"read-more-box\" href=\"/about-us\">Learn more</a></p>\n</div>\n      \n                        </div>\n                    </div>\n                                                                                                                                                                                            <div class=\"node-sidebar col-sm-3\">\n                                                                       <div class=\"row\">\n                                        <div class=\"node-content col-sm-10\">\n                        \n                                                    <div class=\"node-title\">\n                                                                    <h2 class=\"node-title\">Effective Digital Curriculum</h2>\n                                                            </div>\n                                                \n                        <div class=\"content\">\n                            \n            <div class=\"field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field--item\"><p>What do we mean by effective digital curriculum?</p>\n\n<p>Yes, our digital curriculum is designed to meet standards, rigorous, and based on leading research.&nbsp;Yes, it includes direct instruction, practice and application, and formative and summative assessment. All of these things are a given—you expect them. &nbsp;</p>\n\n<p>But that's not all we mean when we talk about effective digital curriculum. &nbsp;</p>\n\n<p>To us, effective&nbsp;means that more learning happens.&nbsp;Our digital&nbsp;curriculum actively engages students in their&nbsp;learning and integrates supports and scaffolds to guide&nbsp;all students in achieving success.</p></div>\n
